<script type="text/javascript">
    var dom = document.getElementById("container");
    var myChart = echarts.init(dom);
    var app = {};

    var option;

    var data = [];
    var geoCoordMap ={};
    var testData = {};

    $.when(
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                dataType: "json",
                async: false,
                url: "/admin/echarts/getCoordinates",
                success:function(responseDate){
                    geoCoordMap = responseDate;
                }
            }),
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                async: false,
                url: "/admin/echarts/getStudentData",
                success:function (response){
                    data = response;
                }
            })
    ).done(function (){

        var convertData = function (data) {
            var res = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                var geoCoord = geoCoordMap[data[i].name];
                if (geoCoord) {
                    res.push({
                        name: data[i].name,
                        value: geoCoord.concat(data[i].value)
                    });
                }
            }
            return res;
        };

        function renderItem(params, api) {
            var coords = [
                [116.7, 39.53],
                [103.73, 36.03],
                [112.91, 27.87],
                [120.65, 28.01],
                [119.57, 39.95]
            ];
            var points = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < coords.length; i++) {
                points.push(api.coord(coords[i]));
            }
            var color = api.visual('color');

            return {
                type: 'polygon',
                shape: {
                    points: echarts.graphic.clipPointsByRect(points, {
                        x: params.coordSys.x,
                        y: params.coordSys.y,
                        width: params.coordSys.width,
                        height: params.coordSys.height
                    })
                },
                style: api.style({
                    fill: color,
                    stroke: echarts.color.lift(color)
                })
            };
        }

        option = {
            backgroundColor: 'transparent',
            title: {
                text: '智易平台用户分布',

                    type: 'custom',
                    coordinateSystem: 'bmap',
                    renderItem: renderItem,
                    itemStyle: {
                        opacity: 0.5
                    },
                    animation: false,
                    silent: true,
                    data: [0],
                    z: -10
                }
            ]
        };

        if (option && typeof option === 'object') {
            myChart.setOption(option);
        }

后端controller

用户登录时更新所在地ip地址

通过百度开放接口

properties配置项

baiduAK=你自己的百度ak
baidu.find.address=https://api.map.baidu.com/location/ip?ak=secret&ip=ipaddress&coor=bd09ll

//UserController
package com.wehbmu.campus_market.controller.home;

import com.alibaba.fastjson.JSONObject;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.annotion.ValidateEntity;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.admin.EchartsService;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.util.StringUtil;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.apache.commons.lang3.StringUtils;
import org.hibernate.tool.schema.internal.exec.ScriptTargetOutputToUrl;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.PropertySource;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.mail.MailSender;
import org.springframework.mail.SimpleMailMessage;
import org.springframework.mail.javamail.JavaMailSender;
import org.springframework.mail.javamail.MimeMessageHelper;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Controller;
import org.springframework.ui.Model;
import org.springframework.util.CollectionUtils;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import com.wehbmu.campus_market.bean.CodeMsg;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.bean.PageBean;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.bean.Result;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.constant.SessionConstant;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.entity.common.Goods;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.entity.common.News;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.entity.common.Student;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.common.GoodsCategoryService;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.common.GoodsService;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.common.NewsService;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.common.StudentService;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.util.SessionUtil;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.util.ValidateEntityUtil;
import org.springframework.web.multipart.MultipartFile;

import javax.mail.MessagingException;
import javax.mail.internet.MimeMessage;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.net.InetAddress;
import java.net.MalformedURLException;
import java.net.UnknownHostException;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.text.ParseException;
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
import java.util.*;

/**
 * 前台首页控制器
 * @author Hmoumou
 *
 */
@RequestMapping("/home/index")
@Controller
@Slf4j
@PropertySource(value = "application.properties",encoding = "UTF-8")
public class IndexController {

    //发送邮件
   @Autowired
   private JavaMailSender javaMailSender;

   @Autowired
   private GoodsService goodsService;
   @Autowired
   private GoodsCategoryService goodsCategoryService;
   @Autowired
   private StudentService studentService;
   @Autowired
   private NewsService newsService;
   @Autowired
   private JavaMailSender mailSender;
   @Autowired
   private EchartsService echartsService;

   @Value("${spring.mail.username}")
   private String emailSendForm;

   @Value("${baiduAK}")
   private String baiduAK;

   @Value("${baidu.find.address}")
   private String baiduFindAddressUrl;

   /**
    * 省市行政编码*/
   @Value("${Administrative.code}")
   private String[] administrativeCode;

   /**
    * 用户登录页面
    * @param model
    * @return
    */
   @RequestMapping(value="/login",method=RequestMethod.GET)
   public String login(Model model){
      return "home/index/login";
   }

   /**
    * 退出登录
    * @return
    */
   @RequestMapping(value="/logout",method=RequestMethod.GET)
   public String logout(){
      SessionUtil.set(SessionConstant.SESSION_STUDENT_LOGIN_KEY, null);
      return "redirect:login";
   }


   /**
    * @param request
    * @param emailCaptcha
    * @param sn
    * @param password
    * @param mobile
    * @param email
    * 用户注册表单提交
    * @return
    */
   @RequestMapping(value="/register",method=RequestMethod.POST)
   @ResponseBody
   public Result<Boolean> register(
         HttpServletRequest request,
         @RequestParam(value = "emailCaptcha") String emailCaptcha,
         @RequestParam(value = "sn")String sn,
         @RequestParam(value = "password")String password,
         @RequestParam(value = "mobile")String mobile,
         @RequestParam(value = "email")String email
   ) throws IOException {
//    校验注册邮箱唯一
      Student findByEmail =this.studentService.findByEmail(email);
      if (findByEmail != null){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_EMAIL_NOTONLY_ERROR);
      }

//    校验注册手机唯一性
      Student findByMobile = this.studentService.findByMobile(mobile);
      if (findByMobile != null){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_MOBILE_NOTONLY_ERROR);
      }

      Student student = new Student();
      student.setSn(sn);
      student.setPassword(password);
      student.setMobile(mobile);
      student.setEmail(email);
      student.setNickname(sn);
      student.setQq("未完善");
      student.setSchool("未完善");
      student.setAcademy("未完善");
      student.setGrade("未完善");

      /*获取用户注册ip地址*/
      String ipAddress = this.studentService.getRegionIpAddress();
      student.setIpaddress(ipAddress);

      /*通过用户的注册ip获取注册地址*/
      JSONObject regionRealAddress = this.studentService.getRegionRealAddress(ipAddress, baiduAK);
      String realAddress = regionRealAddress.get("city").toString();
      student.setRegionaddress(realAddress);

//    邮箱验证码校验
      if (StringUtils.isEmpty(request.getSession().getAttribute("user_register").
            toString()) || emailCaptcha.equals(request.getSession().
            getAttribute("user_register").toString())){
         /*前面的验证均通过后，根据realAddress，在分布图数据中进行+1操作*/
         this.echartsService.addDistributionValueByRealAddress(realAddress);
         CodeMsg validate = ValidateEntityUtil.validate(student);
         if(validate.getCode() != CodeMsg.SUCCESS.getCode()){
            return Result.error(validate);
         }
         //基本验证通过
         if(studentService.findBySn(student.getSn()) != null){
            return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_REGISTER_SN_EXIST);
         }

         /*判断注册的邮箱和之前接收验证码的邮箱是否一致*/
         String user_register_email = (String) request.getSession().getAttribute("user_register_email");
         if (!email.equals(user_register_email)){
            return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_EMAIL_NOT_SAME);
         }
         student = studentService.save(student);
         if(student == null){
            return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_REGISTER_ERROR);
         }

         //表示注册成功，此时将用户信息放入session
         SessionUtil.set(SessionConstant.SESSION_STUDENT_LOGIN_KEY, student);
         return Result.success(true);

      }
      return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_EMAIL_CAPTCHA_ERROR);
   }

   /**
    * 用户登录表单提交
    * @param sn
    * @param password
    * @return
    */
   @RequestMapping(value="/login",method=RequestMethod.POST)
   @ResponseBody
   public Result<Boolean> login(
         @RequestParam(name="sn",required=true)String sn,
         @RequestParam(name="password",required=true)String password,
         @RequestParam(name = "captcha",required = true)String captcha,
         HttpServletRequest request
   ) throws IOException {
//    验证验证码是否为空
      if (StringUtils.isEmpty(captcha)){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.CAPTCHA_EMPTY);
      }
//    从session中获取验证码
      Object loginCaptcha = request.getSession().getAttribute("admin_login");
      if (loginCaptcha == null){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.SESSION_EXPIRED);
      }
//    判断验证码是否一致
      if (!captcha.equalsIgnoreCase(loginCaptcha.toString())){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.CAPTCHA_ERROR);
      }

      Student student = studentService.findBySn(sn);
      if(student == null){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_REGISTER_SN_EXIST);
      }
      student = studentService.save(student);
      if(student == null){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_SN_NO_EXIST);
      }
      //表示学号存在，验证密码是否正确
      if(!student.getPassword().equals(password)){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_PASSWORD_ERROR);
      }
      //验证用户状态是否被冻结
      if(student.getStatus() != Student.STUDENT_STATUS_ENABLE){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_UNABLE);
      }

      /*获取用户登录ip地址*/
      String ipAddress = this.studentService.getRegionIpAddress();

      /*通过用户的登录ip获取登录地址*/
      JSONObject regionRealAddress = this.studentService.getRegionRealAddress(ipAddress, baiduAK);
      String realAddress = regionRealAddress.get("city").toString();

      /*登录的时候判断是否和注册地址一致，一致则无改动
       * 若不一致，则在vesper_distribution表中-1，并在对应地区的value中+1*/

      /*根据学号获取用户注册地址*/
      String oldAddress = this.studentService.getRegionAddressBySn(sn);
      /*判断目前登录地址是否和数据库中存储的上一次登录地一致*/
      if (!oldAddress.equals(realAddress)){
         /*当两次地址不一致时，更新地址和登录的外网IP*/
         this.studentService.updateLastestAddressAndIPBySn(sn,realAddress,ipAddress);
         /*获取上一次登录地址分布图 总人数，并-1*/
         this.echartsService.reduceOneByOldAddress(oldAddress);
         /*获取本次登录地址分布图 总人数，并+1*/
         this.echartsService.addOneByRealAddress(realAddress);
      }

      //表示一切都符合，此时将用户信息放入session
      SessionUtil.set(SessionConstant.SESSION_STUDENT_LOGIN_KEY, student);

      return Result.success(true);
   }

   /**
    * 发送邮件
    * @param email
    * @param request
    * @return
    */
   @PostMapping("/sendCaptcha")
   public ResponseEntity<String> sendCaptcha(
         @RequestParam(value="email") String email,
         HttpServletRequest request
   ){
      /*首先校验邮箱唯一性*/
      //    校验注册邮箱唯一
      Student findByEmail =this.studentService.findByEmail(email);
      if (findByEmail != null){
         return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST).build();
      }
      int captcha = (int) ((Math.random() * 9 + 1) * 100000);
      // 发送邮件
      SimpleMailMessage message = new SimpleMailMessage();
      message.setSubject("欢迎注册校园二手信息共享平台，请查收验证码");
      message.setText("尊敬的用户,您好:\n"
            + "\n本次请求的邮件验证码为:" + captcha + ",本验证码5分钟内有效，请及时输入。（请勿泄露此验证码）\n"
            + "\n如非本人操作，请忽略该邮件。\n(这是一封自动发送的邮件，请不要直接回复）");
      message.setFrom(emailSendForm);
      message.setTo(email);
      javaMailSender.send(message);
      //将验证码存入session
      request.getSession().setAttribute("user_register",captcha);
      //将接收验证码的邮箱存入session
      request.getSession().setAttribute("user_register_email",email);
      log.info("验证码发送成功,user_register" + ",value="+ captcha);
      return ResponseEntity.ok().build();
   }

   /**
    * 重置密码
    * @param email
    * @return
    */
   @GetMapping("/resetPasswordCheckEmail")
   @ResponseBody
   public Result<Boolean> resetPasswordCheckEmail(@RequestParam(value = "email")String email){
      Student studentServiceByEmail = this.studentService.findByEmail(email);
      if (studentServiceByEmail != null){
         return Result.success(true);
      }else {
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.HOME_STUDENT_EMAIL_NO_REGISTER_ERROR);
      }
   }

   /**
    * 发送重置密码连接
    * @param email
    * @param request
    * @return
    * @throws MessagingException
    * @throws ParseException
    */
   @PostMapping("/sendResetPasswordLink")
   @ResponseBody
   public ResponseEntity<String> sendResetPasswordLink(
         @RequestParam(value = "email")String email,
         HttpServletRequest request
   ) throws MessagingException, ParseException {
      /*项目的服务器地址*/
      String serverAddress = request.getScheme() + "://" + request.getServerName() + ":" + request.getServerPort();
      /*根据email查询用户相对应的学号*/
      Student student = this.studentService.findByEmail(email);
      String sn = student.getSn();

      String resetPasswordStartTime = StringUtil.getFormatterDate(new Date(), "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
      Date dateStart = StringUtil.getFormatterDateFromString(resetPasswordStartTime, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
      long operateTimeStart = dateStart.getTime();
      /*将开始申请重置密码的操作时间存入session
      * 根据邮箱，找寻对应的用户学号存入session
      * */
      request.getSession().setAttribute("resetPassword_operateTime",operateTimeStart);
      request.getSession().setAttribute("resetPassword_sn",sn);

      /*重置密码接口链接*/
      String resetPasswordLink = serverAddress + "/home/index/resetPasswordByEmailIndex";
      /*发送重置密码链接的邮件*/
      MimeMessage mimeMessage = mailSender.createMimeMessage();
      MimeMessageHelper helper = new MimeMessageHelper(mimeMessage);
      helper.setFrom(emailSendForm);
      helper.setTo(email);
      helper.setSubject("智易平台密码重置");
      helper.setText("您正在为账号"+email.toString()+"进行密码重置操作。该链接30min内有效，请即时更改。点此链接进行密码重置"+resetPasswordLink);
      mailSender.send(mimeMessage);
      return ResponseEntity.ok().build();
   }

   @RequestMapping("/resetPasswordByEmailIndex")
   public String resetPasswordByEmailIndex(HttpServletRequest request){
      return "home/index/resetPasswordByEmailIndex";
   }

   @PostMapping("/resetPassword")
   @ResponseBody
   public Result<Boolean> resetPassword(
         HttpServletRequest request,
         @RequestParam(value = "sn")String sn,
         @RequestParam(value = "password")String password,
         @RequestParam(value = "passwordAgain")String passwordAgina,
         @RequestParam(value = "captcha")String captcha) throws ParseException {
      /*获取session中之前存入的sn学号和开始申请重置密码的操作时间operateTime*/
      String resetPassword_sn = request.getSession().getAttribute("resetPassword_sn").toString();
      long resetPassword_operateTime = (long) request.getSession().getAttribute("resetPassword_operateTime");
      /*获取session中验证码*/
      String captchaSession =(String) request.getSession().getAttribute("admin_login");
      /*获取当前操作时间*/
      String resetPassword_end = StringUtil.getFormatterDate(new Date(),"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
      Date resetPassword_endT = StringUtil.getFormatterDateFromString(resetPassword_end,"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
      long resetPassword_endTime = resetPassword_endT.getTime();
      /*计算从开始申请重置密码到开始重置的时间差min*/
      int minutes = (int) ((resetPassword_endTime - resetPassword_operateTime) / (1000 * 60));
      /*判断操作是否超时*/
      if (!(minutes >= 0 && minutes <= 30)){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.USER_PASSWORD_RESET_TIMEOUT);
      }
      /*判断学号是否与邮箱对应*/
      if (!resetPassword_sn.equals(sn)){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.USER_PASSWORD_RESET_SN_ERROR);
      }
      /*判断两个密码是否一致*/
      if (!password.equals(passwordAgina)){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.USER_PASSWORD_RESET_NOTSAME);
      }

      /*判断验证码是否一致*/
      if (!(captcha.toUpperCase()).equals(captchaSession.toUpperCase())){
         return Result.error(CodeMsg.CAPTCHA_ERROR);
      }
      /*根据学号重置密码*/
      this.studentService.updateStuPasswordBySn(sn,password);

      return Result.success(true);
   }

   /**
    * @return
    * 返回用户当前所在地
    * */
   @RequestMapping("/getProviceAndCity")
   @ResponseBody
   public HashMap<Object,Object> getWeatherDataAndAddress() throws IOException {

      /*获取用户ip地址*/
      Student loginedStudent = (Student)SessionUtil.get(SessionConstant.SESSION_STUDENT_LOGIN_KEY);
      String ipAddress = loginedStudent.getIpaddress();

      /*获取当前用户所在位置，省市两级*/
      /*通过用户的注册ip获取注册地址*/
      JSONObject regionRealAddress = this.studentService.getRegionRealAddress(ipAddress, baiduAK);

      HashMap<Object, Object> map = new HashMap<>();
      map.put("nowProvince",regionRealAddress.get("province"));
      map.put("nowCity",regionRealAddress.get("city"));
      return map;
   }

   /**
    * 根据城市行政编码返回天气信息
    * @param cityBianMa
    * @return
    */
   @RequestMapping("/getWeatherData")
   @ResponseBody
   public HashMap<String,Object> getWeatherData(@RequestParam(value = "cityBianMa")String cityBianMa) throws IOException {
      JSONObject weatherResult =  this.studentService.getWeatherData(cityBianMa,baiduAK);
      JSONObject location = (JSONObject) weatherResult.get("location");
      JSONObject now = (JSONObject) weatherResult.get("now");
      HashMap<String, Object> map = new HashMap<>();
      map.put("weatherCity",location.get("city"));
      map.put("weatherData",now.get("text"));
      map.put("cityName",location.get("name"));

      return map;
   }

}

package com.wehbmu.campus_market.service.common;
/**
 * 学生信息操作service
 */
import com.alibaba.fastjson.JSON;
import com.alibaba.fastjson.JSONObject;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.constant.SessionConstant;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.util.SessionUtil;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.PropertySource;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Example;
import org.springframework.data.domain.ExampleMatcher;
import org.springframework.data.domain.ExampleMatcher.GenericPropertyMatchers;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort.Direction;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

import com.wehbmu.campus_market.bean.PageBean;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.dao.common.StudentDao;
import com.wehbmu.campus_market.entity.common.Student;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;

import java.io.*;
import java.net.*;
import java.util.*;

@Service
@Transactional
@PropertySource(value = "json.properties",encoding = "UTF-8")
public class StudentService {

   @Autowired
   private StudentDao studentDao;

   /*省市行政编码*/
   @Value("${Administrative.code}")
   private String[] countryCode;

   /**
    * 根据学号查询
    * @param sn
    * @return
    */
   public Student findBySn(String sn){
      return studentDao.findBySn(sn);
   }

   /**
    * 根据id查找
    * @param id
    * @return
    */
   public Student findById(Long id){
      return studentDao.find(id);
   }

   /**
    * 学生修改/编辑，当传入id时则为编辑，若id为空则为添加
    * @param student
    * @return
    */
   public Student save(Student student){
      return studentDao.save(student);
   }

   /**
    * 搜索学生列表
    * @param pageBean
    * @param student
    * @return
    */
   public PageBean<Student> findlist(PageBean<Student> pageBean,Student student){
      ExampleMatcher exampleMatcher = ExampleMatcher.matching();
      exampleMatcher = exampleMatcher.withMatcher("sn", GenericPropertyMatchers.contains());
      exampleMatcher = exampleMatcher.withIgnorePaths("status");
      Example<Student> example = Example.of(student, exampleMatcher);
      Sort sort = Sort.by(Direction.DESC, "createTime");
      PageRequest pageable = PageRequest.of(pageBean.getCurrentPage()-1, pageBean.getPageSize(), sort);
      Page<Student> findAll = studentDao.findAll(example, pageable);
      pageBean.setContent(findAll.getContent());
      pageBean.setTotal(findAll.getTotalElements());
      pageBean.setTotalPage(findAll.getTotalPages());
      return pageBean;
   }

   /**
    * 根据id删除
    * @param id
    */
   public void delete(Long id){
      studentDao.deleteById(id);
   }

   /**
    * 获取学生总数
    * @return
    */
   public long total(){
      return studentDao.count();
   }

   /**
    * @param email
    * 校验邮箱唯一性
    * @return
    */
   public Student findByEmail(String email) {
     return this.studentDao.findByEmail(email);
   }

   /**
    * @param mobile
    * 校验注册手机唯一性
    * @return
    */
   public Student findByMobile(String mobile) {
      return studentDao.findByMobile(mobile);
   }

   /**
    * 保存用户的学生证信息
    * 通过用户的id
    * @return
    */
   public void updateStuCardImg(String stuCardImg, Long stuId) {
      this.studentDao.updateStuCardImg(stuCardImg,stuId);
   }

   /**
    * 获取注册用户的ip地址
    */
    public String getRegionIpAddress() throws IOException {
      /*像网站发送请求，该网站可以返回本地的外网ip*/
      JSONObject json = new JSONObject();
      json.put("orderId","2021061015241733858019");
      String urls = "http://pv.sohu.com/cityjson";
      URL url = new URL(urls);
      /*打开和url间的连接*/
      HttpURLConnection connection = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
      PrintWriter out = null;
      /*请求方式*/
      connection.setRequestMethod("GET");
      /*设置通用请求属性*/
      connection.setRequestProperty("accept","*/*");
      connection.setRequestProperty("connection","Keep-Alive");
      connection.setRequestProperty("Content-Type","application/json;charset=utf-8");
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输出流*/
      connection.connect();
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输入流*/
      InputStream inputStream = connection.getInputStream();
      /*构造字符流缓存*/
      BufferedReader bufferedReader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(inputStream));
      String siteInfo = bufferedReader.readLine();
      JSONObject map = JSON.parseObject(siteInfo.substring(siteInfo.lastIndexOf("{"),siteInfo.lastIndexOf("}")+1));
      /*关流*/
      inputStream.close();
      /*断开连接*/
      connection.disconnect();

      String ipAddress = (String) map.get("cip");
      return ipAddress;
   }


   /**
    * 通过用户的注册ip获取注册地址
    * @param ipAddress  前期获得的注册用户外网IP
    * @param baiduAK  百度开发者
    */
   public JSONObject getRegionRealAddress(String ipAddress,String baiduAK) throws IOException {
      /*向网站发起请求*/
      JSONObject json = new JSONObject();
      json.put("orderId","2021061015241733858078");
//    https://api.map.baidu.com/location/ip?ak=secret&ip=ipaddress&coor=bd09ll

      String baiduFindAddressUrl = "https://api.map.baidu.com/location/ip?ak="+baiduAK+"&ip="+ipAddress+"&coor=bd09ll";

      URL url = new URL(baiduFindAddressUrl);
      /*打开和url间的连接*/
      HttpURLConnection connection = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
      PrintWriter out = null;
      /*设置请求方式*/
      connection.setRequestMethod("GET");
      /*设置通用请求属性*/
      connection.setRequestProperty("accept","*/*");
      connection.setRequestProperty("connection","Keep-Alive");
      connection.setRequestProperty("Content-Type","application/json;charset=utf-8");
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输出流*/
      connection.connect();
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输入流*/
      InputStream inputStream = connection.getInputStream();
      /*构造字符流缓存*/
      BufferedReader bufferedReader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(inputStream));
      String readLine = bufferedReader.readLine();

      JSONObject map = (JSONObject) JSON.parseObject(readLine).get("content");
      JSONObject address = (JSONObject) map.get("address_detail");
      /*String realAddress = map1.get("city").toString();
      String province = map1.get("province").toString();*/
      /*关流*/
      inputStream.close();
      /*断开连接*/
      connection.disconnect();
      return address;
   }

   /**
    * 根据学号重置密码
    * @param password
    * @param sn 学号
    */
   public void updateStuPasswordBySn(String sn, String password) {
      this.studentDao.updateStuPasswordBySn(sn,password);
   }

   /**
    * 检索用户信息
    */
    public List<Student> findAll() {
      return this.studentDao.findAll();
    }

   /**
    * 根据学号获取用户注册地址
    * @param sn
    * @return
    */
   public String getRegionAddressBySn(String sn) {
      return  this.studentDao.getRegionAddressBySn(sn);
   }


   /**
    * 当两次地址不一致时，更新地址和登录的外网IP
    * @param sn
    * @param realAddress
    * @param ipAddress
    */
   public void updateLastestAddressAndIPBySn(String sn, String realAddress, String ipAddress) {
      this.studentDao.updateLastestAddressAndIPBySn(sn,realAddress,ipAddress);
   }


   /**
    * 根据城市行政编码和baiduAK返回当地的天气信息
    * @param cityBianMa
    * @param baiduAK
    */
   public JSONObject getWeatherData(String cityBianMa, String baiduAK) throws IOException {

      /*向网站发起请求*/
      JSONObject json = new JSONObject();
      json.put("orderId","2021061015241733858078");
//    http://api.map.baidu.com/weather/v1/?district_id=222405&data_type=all&ak=你的ak

      String baiduGetWeatherData = "http://api.map.baidu.com/weather/v1/?district_id="+cityBianMa+"&data_type=all&ak="+baiduAK;

      URL url = new URL(baiduGetWeatherData);
      /*打开和url间的连接*/
      HttpURLConnection connection = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
      PrintWriter out = null;
      /*设置请求方式*/
      connection.setRequestMethod("GET");
      /*设置通用请求属性*/
      connection.setRequestProperty("accept","*/*");
      connection.setRequestProperty("connection","Keep-Alive");
      connection.setRequestProperty("Content-Type","application/json;charset=utf-8");
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输出流*/
      connection.connect();
      /*获取URLConnection对象对应的输入流*/
      InputStream inputStream = connection.getInputStream();
      /*构造字符流缓存*/
      BufferedReader bufferedReader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(inputStream));
      String readLine = bufferedReader.readLine();

      JSONObject weatherResult = (JSONObject) JSON.parseObject(readLine).get("result");

      /*关流*/
      inputStream.close();
      /*断开连接*/
      connection.disconnect();
      return weatherResult;

   }
}

@Controller

public class EchartsController {

    @Autowired
    private EchartsService echartsService;

    /**
     * 全国各省市坐标json数据
     */
    @Value("${Geographic.Coordinates}")
    private String coordinates;

    @RequestMapping("/index")
    public String index(){
        return "admin/echarts/distribution";
    }

    /**
     * @return
     * 获取全国各省市的json坐标数据
     */
    @RequestMapping(value = "/getCoordinates",produces = "application/json;charset=utf-8")
    @ResponseBody
    public String getCoordinates(){
        return coordinates;
    }

    /**
     * @return
     * 从数据库获取用户注册地址消息
     */
    @RequestMapping(value = "/getStudentData",produces = "application/json;charset=utf-8")
    @ResponseBody
    public List<Distribution> getStudentData(){
        return this.echartsService.getStudentData();
    }

}

-- Table structure for vesper_user
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vesper_user`;
CREATE TABLE `vesper_user`  (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `create_time` datetime NOT NULL,
  `update_time` datetime NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(32) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `head_pic` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `mobile` varchar(12) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(32) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `sex` int(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` int(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `username` varchar(18) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `role_id` bigint(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `ipaddress` char(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `UK_btsosjytrl4hu7fnm1intcpo8`(`username`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `FKg09b8o67eu61st68rv6nk8npj`(`role_id`) USING BTREE,
  CONSTRAINT `vesper_user_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`role_id`) REFERENCES `vesper_role` (`id`) ON DELETE RESTRICT ON UPDATE RESTRICT
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 11 CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_general_ci ROW_FORMAT = Dynamic;
